#Scripted Variables moved to their own file for easier editing
giga_megaview_vat_01 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {}
}

giga_the_vat_01_pb_000_100 = { potential = { is_scope_type = megastructure exists = from from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } check_variable = { which = the_vat_01_pixel value >= 1 } } allow = {} effect = {} } 
giga_vat_01_timer = { potential = { is_scope_type = megastructure exists = from from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use } allow = {} effect = {} }
#This is now the sole thing tracking to tell you how many of X things you're growing in vat 1
giga_vat_01_grow_amount = { 
	potential = { 
		is_scope_type = megastructure 
		exists = from 
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } 
		OR = { 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4 
		} 
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use 
		check_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_amount value >= 1 } 
	} 
	allow = {} 
	effect = {} 
}
#This is now the sole button for tracking subtractions of variabls for vat
giga_vat_01_grow_minus = {#optimized the length of this bad boy
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_amount value = 1 }
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_MINUS_1"
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_amount
				value < 999
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|food| }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_no_live_god"
			NAND = { 
				has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_10
				from = {
				 	has_country_flag = giga_vat_live_god 
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_1"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|food| }# |WHO|this
			add_resource = { energy = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|energy| }# |WHO|this
		}
	} 
}

giga_vat_01_grow_cancel = { #Cancels the queue
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_cancel_refund|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_cancel_refund|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_10}
			from = {
				add_resource = { exotic_gases = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_cancel_refund|WHO2|prev|VAT|01|RESOURCE|gas| }
				hidden_effect = { remove_country_flag = giga_vat_live_god }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			giga_the_vat_01_clear = yes
		}
	}
}

#Ether Drake
giga_vat_01_grow_01 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_01_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_01_energy_cost }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_leviathan_slain_dragon"
			from = { has_country_flag = giga_vat_can_clone_dragon }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_01_cost_food value = @grow_01_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_01_cost_energy value = @grow_01_energy_cost}
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_01
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_01_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_time value = @grow_01_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.14001 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_01
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|01|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|01|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|09|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|09|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

#Toxic god
giga_vat_01_grow_10 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_10_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_10_energy_cost }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_no_live_god"
		 	from = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = giga_vat_live_god }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_vat_4"
		 	is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_leviathan_toxic_god"
			from = { has_country_flag = giga_vat_can_clone_toxic_god }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_01_cost_food value = @grow_10_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_01_cost_energy value = @grow_10_energy_cost}
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_01_cost_gas value = @grow_10_gas_cost }
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_10
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_01_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_time value = @grow_10_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.14001 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_10
		}
		from = {
			set_country_flag = giga_vat_live_god
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|10|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|10|RESOURCE|energy| }
			add_resource = { exotic_gases = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|10|RESOURCE|gas| }
		}
	}
}

giga_the_vat_02_pb_000_100 = { potential = { is_scope_type = megastructure exists = from from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } check_variable = { which = the_vat_02_pixel value >= 1 } } allow = {} effect = {} } 
giga_vat_02_timer = { potential = { is_scope_type = megastructure exists = from from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use } allow = {} effect = {} }
giga_vat_02_grow_amount = { 
	potential = { 
		is_scope_type = megastructure 
		exists = from 
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } 
		OR = { 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4 
		} 
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use 
		check_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_amount value >= 1 } 
	} 
	allow = {} 
	effect = {} 
}

giga_vat_02_grow_minus = {#optimized the lenght of this bad boy
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_02_grow_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_amount value = 1 }
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_MINUS_1"
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|02|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|02|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_02_grow_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_02_grow_amount
				value < 999
			}
			exists = from
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_07}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_08}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_09}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
			}
		}

	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_1"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|02|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|02|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_02_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_02_cost_food value = @grow_06_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_02_cost_energy value = @grow_06_energy_cost}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_02_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_time value = @grow_06_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.24001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_amount = { 
	potential = { 
		is_scope_type = megastructure 
		exists = from 
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } 
		OR = { 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4 
		} 
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use 
		check_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_amount value >= 1 } 
	} 
	allow = {} 
	effect = {} 
}

giga_vat_03_grow_minus = {#optimized the lenght of this bad boy
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_03_grow_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_amount value = 1 }
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_MINUS_1"
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|03|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|03|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_03_grow_amount
				value < 999
			}
			exists = from
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_07}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_08}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_09}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
			}
		}

	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_1"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|03|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|03|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_03_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_03_cost_food value = @grow_06_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_03_cost_energy value = @grow_06_energy_cost}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_03_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_time value = @grow_06_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.34001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|food| }

# Swarm Warrior
giga_vat_03_grow_07 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_03_cost_food value = @grow_07_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_03_cost_energy value = @grow_07_energy_cost}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_03_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_time value = @grow_07_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.34001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|07|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|07|RESOURCE|energy| }

giga_vat_04_grow_amount = { 
	potential = { 
		is_scope_type = megastructure 
		exists = from 
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } 
		OR = { 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4 
		} 
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use 
		check_variable = { which = giga_vat_04_grow_amount value >= 1 } 
	} 
	allow = {} 
	effect = {} 
}

giga_vat_04_grow_minus = {#optimized the lenght of this bad boy
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {

giga_vat_04_grow_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_04_grow_amount
				value < 999
			}
			exists = from
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_06}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_07}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_08}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_09}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
			}
		}

	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_1"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_04_grow_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|04|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|04|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_04_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_04_cost_food value = @grow_06_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_04_cost_energy value = @grow_06_energy_cost}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_04_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_04_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_04_grow_time value = @grow_06_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.44001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_amount = { 
	potential = { 
		is_scope_type = megastructure 
		exists = from 
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } 
		OR = { 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4 
		} 
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use 
		check_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount value >= 1 } 
	} 
	allow = {} 
	effect = {} 
}

giga_vat_05_grow_minus = {#optimized the lenght of this bad boy
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount value = 1 }
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_MINUS_1"
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|05|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|05|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount
				value < 999
			}
			exists = from
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_07}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_08}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_09}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
			}
		}

	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_1"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|05|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|05|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_10 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
	}
	allow = {	
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount
				value < 989
			}
			exists = from
		} if = { 
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost mult = 10 }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost mult = 10}
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_07}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost mult = 10}
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost mult = 10}
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_08}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost mult = 10}
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost mult = 10}
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_09}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost mult = 10}
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost mult = 10}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_10"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount value = 10 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -10 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|05|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = -10 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|05|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_05_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_05_cost_food value = @grow_06_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_05_cost_energy value = @grow_06_energy_cost}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_05_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_time value = @grow_06_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.54001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_amount = {

		exists = from 
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } 
		OR = { 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4 
		} 
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use 
		check_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_amount value >= 1 } 
	} 
	allow = {} 
	effect = {} 
}

giga_vat_06_grow_minus = {#optimized the lenght of this bad boy
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_06_grow_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_amount value = 1 }
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_MINUS_1"
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|06|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|06|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_06_grow_amount
				value < 999
			}
			exists = from
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_06}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_07}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_08}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_09}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
			}
		}

	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_1"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|06|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|06|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

			from = {

				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost mult = 10}
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_08}

		}
	}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_06_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_06_cost_food value = @grow_06_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_06_cost_energy value = @grow_06_energy_cost}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_06_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_time value = @grow_06_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.64001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_amount = { 
	potential = { 
		is_scope_type = megastructure 
		exists = from 
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } 
		OR = { 
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4 
		} 
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use 
		check_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_amount value >= 1 } 
	} 
	allow = {} 
	effect = {} 
}

giga_vat_07_grow_minus = {#optimized the lenght of this bad boy
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_07_grow_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_amount value = 1 }
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_MINUS_1"
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|07|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|07|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_07_grow_amount
				value < 999
			}
			exists = from
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_07}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_08}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_09}
			from = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
				resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
			}
		}

	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = "VAT_GROW_1"
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|07|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = -1 mult = value:giga_vat_grow_cost|WHO2|prev|VAT|07|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_cancel_refund|WHO2|prev|VAT|07|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_cancel_refund|WHO2|prev|VAT|07|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			giga_the_vat_07_clear = yes
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_07_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_07_cost_food value = @grow_06_food_cost }
			set_variable = { which = giga_grow_07_cost_energy value = @grow_06_energy_cost}
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
			set_variable = { which = the_vat_07_pixel value = 1 } # This is so the progress bar isn't broken before the events start firing
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_amount value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_time value = @grow_06_growth_time }
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_vat_events.74001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|food| }
			add_resource = { energy = 1 multiplier = value:giga_vat_initial_grow_cost|GROW|06|RESOURCE|energy| }
		}
	}
}

	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		#from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = planetary_drive_yard_1_fortress
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_megaview_defense_nexus_explain_tooltip_no"
		hidden_trigger = {
			from = {
				is_same_value = prev.owner
				NOT = { has_country_flag = giga_defense_nexus_explain_popup }
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_megaview_defense_nexus_explain_tooltip"
		hidden_effect = { 
			from = {
				set_country_flag = giga_defense_nexus_explain_popup
				country_event = { id = giga_dialog.13403 }
			}
		}
	}
}


giga_megaview_defense_nexus_deploy_now = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		#from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = planetary_drive_yard_1_fortress
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_megaview_defense_nexus_cant_deploy"
		hidden_trigger = {
			from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
			planet = {
				NOR = {
					has_planet_flag = defence_squadron_deployed
					has_planet_flag = giga_defence_squadron_cooldown
					is_occupied_flag = yes
					has_ground_combat = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_megaview_defense_nexus_deploy_tooltip"
		hidden_effect = { 
			planet = {
				planet_event = { id = giga_mega.7001 }
			}
		}
	}
}

giga_megaview_defense_nexus_deploy_system_no = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		#from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = planetary_drive_yard_1_fortress
		planet = { NOT = { has_planet_flag = defense_nexus_deploy_system } }
	}
	allow = {
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_megaview_defense_nexus_deploy_system_yes"
		hidden_effect = { 
			planet = {
				set_planet_flag = defense_nexus_deploy_system
				remove_planet_flag = defense_nexus_deploy_bombard
				remove_planet_flag = defense_nexus_deploy_never
			}
		}
	}
}

giga_megaview_manage = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from # the viewing player
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } # hidden if we're looking at someone else's mega
	}
	allow = {
		# display text when active
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = giga_megaview_manage
			always = yes
		}

		# disable if already open
		hidden_trigger = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				nor = {
					has_country_flag = managing_giga_megastructure
					is_ai = yes # you should not be able to click this for the AI as an observer!
				}
			}
		}

		# only allowed for specific megas
		custom_tooltip_fail = {
			text = giga_megaview_manage_no_options

			is_scope_type = megastructure
			
			giga_is_manageable_mega = yes

			#always = no # re-enable when we're ready for stuff by commenting this line out
		}
	}
	effect = {
		# display text when disabled
		custom_tooltip = giga_megaview_manage

		# open the management window
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				country_event = {
					id = giga_mega_management.001
					scopes = {
						from = root
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

giga_megaview_highlight_toggle_on = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from # the viewing player
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } # hidden if we're looking at someone else's mega
		exists = planet
		planet = {
			not = { has_modifier = giga_highlight_object }
		}
	}
	allow = {
		# display text when active
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = giga_megaview_highlight
			always = yes
		}
	}
	effect = {
		# display text when disabled
		custom_tooltip = giga_megaview_highlight

		# add modifier
		hidden_effect = {
			planet = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = giga_highlight_object
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

giga_megaview_highlight_toggle_off = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from # the viewing player
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } # hidden if we're looking at someone else's mega
		exists = planet
		planet = {
			has_modifier = giga_highlight_object
		}
	}
	allow = {
		# display text when active
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = giga_megaview_highlight
			always = yes
		}
	}
	effect = {
		# display text when disabled
		custom_tooltip = giga_megaview_highlight

		# remove modifier
		hidden_effect = {
			planet = {
				remove_modifier = giga_highlight_object
			}
		}
	}
}

giga_megaview_outliner_toggle_on = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from # the viewing player
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } # hidden if we're looking at someone else's mega
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_outliner_hidden_by_@from }
	}
	allow = {
		# display text when active
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = giga_megaview_outliner
			always = yes
		}
	}
	effect = {
		# display text when disabled
		custom_tooltip = giga_megaview_outliner

		# add flag
		hidden_effect = {
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_outliner_hidden_by_@from
		}
	}
}

giga_megaview_outliner_toggle_off = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from # the viewing player
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner } # hidden if we're looking at someone else's mega
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_outliner_hidden_by_@from
	}
	allow = {
		# display text when active
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = giga_megaview_outliner
			always = yes
		}
	}
	effect = {
		# display text when disabled
		custom_tooltip = giga_megaview_outliner

		# remove flag
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_outliner_hidden_by_@from
		}
	}
}
